package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTBlock) {
                ASTBlock block = (ASTBlock) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                for (int j = 0; j < block.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    if (block.jjtGetChild(j) instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                        addViolation(data, block.jjtGetChild(j));
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForNewObjectInLoop(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForNewObjectInLoop(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForNewObjectInLoop(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForNewObjectInLoop(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForNewObjectInLoop(Node node, Object data) {
        List<ASTAllocationExpression> newObjects = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAllocationExpression.class);
        for (ASTAllocationExpression newObject : newObjects) {
            addViolation(data, newObject);
        }
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTBlock) {
                visit((ASTBlock) child, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTForStatement) {
                visit((ASTForStatement) child, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTBlock) {
                visit((ASTBlock) child, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        addViolation(data, node);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);

    @Override

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// False negative with break in other for-loop
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.SortedSet;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class Message {
    private List<Function<Message, Boolean>> filters;

    public Message(Message message) {}

    private SortedSet<Message> getFilteredMessages(List<Message> messages) {
        final SortedSet<Message> result = new TreeSet<>(messages);
        for (Message element : messages) {
            Message event = new Message(element);
            for (Function<Message, Boolean> filter : filters) {
                if (!filter.apply(event)) {
                    result.remove(element);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return result;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if (isInsideLoop(node)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInsideLoop(ASTConstructorCall node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null) {
            ASTBreakStatement breakNode = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
            if (breakNode == null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            } else {
                if (breakNode.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class).equals(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class))
                        || breakNode.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class).equals(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class))
                        || breakNode.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class).equals(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class))) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.Optional;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTWhileStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null) {

            Optional<ASTBreakStatement> breakStatement = node.getParentsOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class).stream().findFirst();
            if (!breakStatement.isPresent() || breakStatement.get().getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) == null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// False negative with break in other for-loop
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.SortedSet;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class Message {
    private List<Function<Message, Boolean>> filters;

    public Message(Message message) {}

    private SortedSet<Message> getFilteredMessages(List<Message> messages) {
        final SortedSet<Message> result = new TreeSet<>(messages);
        for (Message element : messages) {
            Message event = new Message(element);
            for (Function<Message, Boolean> filter : filters) {
                if (!filter.apply(event)) {
                    result.remove(element);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return result;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    private int loopCounter = 0;

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTWhileStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        loopCounter++;
        super.visit(node, data);
        loopCounter--;
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        loopCounter++;
        super.visit(node, data);
        loopCounter--;
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        loopCounter++;
        super.visit(node, data);
        loopCounter--;
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (loopCounter > 0
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {

    }

            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        final ASTArgumentList argumentList = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
                && (argumentList == null || !(argumentList.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTMethodCall))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        JavaNode currentNode = node.jjtGetParent();
        while (currentNode != null && !(currentNode instanceof ASTCompilationUnit)) {
            if (currentNode instanceof ASTForStatement || currentNode instanceof ASTWhileStatement || currentNode instanceof ASTDoStatement) {
                if (node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
                        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
                        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break;
                }
            }
            currentNode = currentNode.jjtGetParent();
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        checkInfixExpression(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkInfixExpression(Node node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) child;
                for (int j = 0; j < infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                    Node grandChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(j);
                    if (grandChild instanceof ASTConstructorCall) {
                        addViolation(data, grandChild);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a loop condition
        ASTWhileStatement whileParent = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class);
        if (whileParent != null && whileParent.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null

            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTPrefixExpression.class) != null
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpressionNotPlusMinus.class) != null)) {

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a loop condition
        if ((node.getNthParent(2) instanceof ASTWhileStatement 
            || node.getNthParent(2) instanceof ASTForStatement 
            || node.getNthParent(2) instanceof ASTDoStatement)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }
    
    private boolean isLoopParent(ASTConstructorCall node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if (isLoopParent(node)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {

            ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignmentExpression != null) {
                // Check if the assignment is to an array or a collection
                if (assignmentExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) == null
                    && !(assignmentExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
                    && "add".equals(assignmentExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class).getImage()))) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if (isLoopParent(node)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null
            && !(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
            && "add".equals(((ASTMethodCall) node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)).getMethodName()))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
            && !"add".equals(((ASTMethodCall) node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)).getMethodName())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    // ... (no changes to the visit methods for the loop constructs)

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is part of an assignment to an array or a method call to a collection
        boolean isPartOfArrayAssignment = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null;
        boolean isPartOfCollectionAdd = (node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
                                         && "add".equals(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class).getMethodName()));

        if (!isPartOfArrayAssignment && !isPartOfCollectionAdd
            && (node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null

            addViolation(data, node);

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
      
    // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
    if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
        || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
        || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
        // Ignoring assignment to collections
        && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTStatementExpressionList.class) == null) {
      addViolation(data, node);
    }
    return super.visit(node, data);
  }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null
            && !(node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class).getMethod().equals("add"))) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAllocation.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        checkInstantiation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAllocation node, Object data) {
        checkInstantiation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkInstantiation(Object node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAllocation.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAllocation node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNode(Node node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check if the ConstructorCall or ArrayAllocation is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAllocation.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAllocation node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNode(AbstractJavaNode node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAllocation.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if (isInsideLoop(node) && !isInsideSpecificNodes(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if (isInsideLoop(node) && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAllocation node, Object data) {
        if (isInsideLoop(node) && !isInsideSpecificNodes(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInsideLoop(Node node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isInsideSpecificNodes(Node node) {
        return node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) != null
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) != null
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) != null
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) != null
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) != null;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAllocation.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        checkInstantiation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAllocation node, Object data) {
        checkInstantiation(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkInstantiation(AbstractJavaNode node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {

            ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignment == null || !(assignment.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTArrayAccess)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class, ASTArrayAccess.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTArrayAccess node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) != null) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignment.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
            && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        
        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null 
            || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
            && (node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTConstructorCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorCall node, Object data) {
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTCatchClause.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) == null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        // Check if the ConstructorCall is within a method call inside a loop
        if ((node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTForStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTWhileStatement.class) != null
                || node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTDoStatement.class) != null)
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null
                && node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
